border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. simply 仅仅，只是（=only，just，merely...）</strong></p><p 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. V-ing 做主语：</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">being present and offering support and normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">① be present 出席的，到场的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The whole family was <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">present</span></strong></em>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">全家人都<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">在场</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">② offer support and encouragement 提供支持和鼓励</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">offer XX (to sb)  提供，给予...</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">offer advice/help/support... 提出建议/给与帮助/提供支持...</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">offer an opportunity/chance/possibility... 提供机会/可能性...</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 62);box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《恋爱手册》</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. 词链儿：support XX through one's grief 支持别人度过悲伤的时刻</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">① support v. 支持，帮助，援助〔处于困难时期的人〕</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">My wife <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">supported</span></em></strong> me enormously.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我妻子给了我极大的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">支持</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">② 拓展词链儿：work through XX 解决〔问题〕；调整〔情绪〕</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">work through one's grief 从悲伤/哀痛中走出来</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">After someone dies, it can take a long time to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">work through your grief</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有人去世之后，为之悲伤不已的人可能需要很长时间才能<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">从哀痛中走出来</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I was able to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">work through my grief</span></em></strong> both positively and spiritually.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我能够以一种积极的方式，从精神上<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">摆脱悲伤</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Maybe you could <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">work through</span></em></strong> your echo here.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">或许你可以在这里<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">经历</strong>你的死亡轮回。</p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(350.547px, 3487.5px);-webkit-transform: 2px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">au pair/ˌəʊ ˈpeə/(互惠) 源自于法文“互助、互惠”的意思。au pair互惠生，最早起源英、法、德等国，是自发的青年活动：年轻外国人为学习某国语言和体验该国文化寄宿在一个东道主家庭(多为中产阶级)，同时为该家庭做一些看护孩童的工作为西方的一项流行风俗。今天我们就来听听这位澳大利亚的小姐姐聊聊她在西班牙做au pair的经历吧~</p></section></section><section style="margin-left: qualifications are they looking for? I mean, of course, you must be a native English speaker. And what's more? </p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">Well, actually it depends on the family. So, my family just once, I mean, I’m their seventh au pair, they get an au pair every summer every year and they just want someone usually native speaker, but they have had like girls from Sweden or Iceland before, and they just want a girl to speak English with the kids. </em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">But for other families they want someone to really help with the housework and managing the house and things like that. So I actually know a Vietnamese girl who’s an au pair and there are Mexican girls, Russian girls. So yeah, you don't have to be a native speaker and there’s no real qualifications that you need. I guess people…it looks good if you have a degree and you’re interested is enough. </em></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">authentic    </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">BrE /ɔː'θentɪk/   NAmE /ɔ'θɛntɪk/   adj. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.known to be real and genuine and not a copy 真正的；真品的；真迹的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I don’t know if the painting is authentic.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我不知道这幅画是不是真迹。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.true and accurate 真实的；真正的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">an authentic account of life in the desert</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对沙漠生活的真实描述</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the authentic voice of young black Americans</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">年轻美国黑人的真实呼声</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Vietnamese  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">BrE  /ˈvjetnəˈmi:z/   NAmE  /viˌɛtnəˈmiz/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 越南人</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 越南的,越南人的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Dull  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">BrE /dʌl/  NAmE /dʌl/   adj.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">BORING 乏味的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">not interesting or exciting 无趣味的；不刺激的；不生动的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It sounded pretty dull to me. 在我听来，这很无聊。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">其他意思：钝的；呆滞的；阴暗的；迟钝的；</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">curry   </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">BrE /ˈkʌri/  NAmE /ˈkɚri/  n.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a type of food from India, consisting of meat or vegetables in a spicy sauce 咖喱食品</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">chicken curry</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">咖喱鸡</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">get on with继续(干某事)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Right, let's get on with the programme. 好，现在继续节目吧。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">let's get on with the lesson.那我们开始今天的课程吧。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: I'm Dan…</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">大家好，欢迎收听六分钟英语。这个节目带给你有趣的话题，纯正的听力练习和六个非常有用的词汇。我是丹。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: An<span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d I</span>'m Neil. In this programme we'll be discussing the lovely topi<span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">c o</span>f lunch – an<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> wha<span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t o</span>ur lunch choice<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">s</span></span> say abou<span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t u</span>s. So, Dan, what <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">are</em> you doing for lunch today?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我是尼尔。在今天的节目中，我们将讨论关于午餐的有趣话题，以及午餐能够体现我们的什么特点。丹，你今天午餐准备吃什么？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: Ah Neil, <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">are</em> you asking me <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">to</em> join you? You see, I've brough<span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t a</span> sandwich.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">事实上，我只是想引出今天的话题。不好意思。你看，我已经带了一个三明治。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: Oh, a sandwich. Again! How dull. Well, you're no<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">the</strong> only one – a survey from 2012 showe<span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span> third of Britons eat exac<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span>ly the same thing <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">for</em> lunch – every day! An<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> yes, it's mos<span style="text-decoration: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">三明治。又是三明治！太无趣了。也不只有你这样。</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">2012</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: I ha<span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span> curry yesterday.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">昨天我吃的咖喱。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: Well, it'<span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span>lmos<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> lunchtime so we'<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">the</strong> average lunch break in the UK? Is it:a) An hour an<span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span> half, b) 45 minutes or c) 25 minutes?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">快到吃午餐的时间了，我们最好先来看看今天的问题。在英国平均午餐时长是多久？</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">a) </span><span 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Low down and near the horizon hung a great, red sun, far bigger than our sun. Digory felt at once that it was also older than ours: a sun near the end of its life, weary of looking down upon that world. To the left of the sun, and higher up, there was a single star, big and bright. Those were the only two things to be seen in the dark sky; they made a dismal group. And on the earth, in every direction, as far as the eye could reach, there spread a vast city in which there was no living thing to be seen. And all the temples, towers, palaces, pyramids, and bridges cast long, disastrous-looking shadows in the light of that withered sun. Once a great river had flowed through the city, but the water had long since vanished, and it was now only a wide ditch of grey dust.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">往下看，只见一轮比我们的太阳大得多的红太阳在地平线附近，迪格雷立刻就觉得那轮太阳比我们的太阳老：这幕年的太阳已经厌倦于俯视下面的世界。太阳的左上方，有一颗大而亮的星星。黑暗的天空中，残阳和孤星组成了一幅阴郁的画面。地上，有一个不管从哪个方向极目远眺都望不到边际的巨大的城市。城市里不见活动着的人和物。所有的庙宇、楼塔、宫殿、金字塔和桥在衰弱的阳光下投下长长的悲哀的影子。城里曾经有一条河，但河床早已干涸，只刹下一条宽宽的灰色土沟。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你本应该呆在家里享受丰盛大餐的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 是啊。我当时应该提前去买票的，但是现在……</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 但是现在你可以与朋友一起过节。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 对。走，我们找点儿快乐的事去。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: You should have been at home and enjoyed a big meal.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yes. I should have gone to buy the ticket in advance. But now...</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: But now you can stay with friends and enjoy a holiday too.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Right. Let's go and find some fun.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We invited twenty people, but only a handful of them came.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们邀请了20 个人，但只来了___________。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">寥寥数人</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style="text-align: center;"><strong style='max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 词链儿：next to XX 的三种含义：</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;">① 紧邻 </span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We sat <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">next to</span></em></strong> each other. </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">紧挨着</strong>坐在一起。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;">② 仅次于 </span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">Next to</span></em></strong> skiing my <g style="box-sizing: border-box;">favourite </g>sport is skating.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我最喜欢的运动<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">除了</strong>滑雪就是溜冰。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;">③ 与…相比 </span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">Next to </span></em></strong>her, I’m a very poor cook.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">和</strong>她<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">比起来</strong>，我的厨艺太差了。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">Next to</span></em></strong> <g style="box-sizing: border-box;">her </g>I felt like a <span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><em>fraud</em></span>.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">和</strong>她<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">相比</strong>，我觉得自己是<strong>滥竽充数</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">*...is nothing <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">next to</span></em></strong> you <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">与</strong>你<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">相比</strong>，什么都不是。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. the sun in the midday hue 正午耀眼的阳光</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">midday 中午，正午</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">midday sun 正午阳光</p><p style="text-align: center;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img js_insertlocalimg" data-ratio="0.6609375" data-s="300,640" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfMBRicgibt2dumCQZz7vnxKib6uSSa3SOXiawalsJmQbAPx6KDxMDrrnvRosMicQ6GtMAcV1roOfEZT9A/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="640" style=""/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the full heat of the <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">midday</span></em></strong> sun</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">正午</strong>烈日的酷热</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">hue /hjuː/ 颜色；色调；色度</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">His face took on an unhealthy whitish <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">hue</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他的脸上透出一丝病态的苍白。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4.  词链儿：have nothing left to.../ there is nothing left to...</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">没有什么可以...的了</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">have nothing left to</span></em></strong> wish for. </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">再也没什么</strong>想要<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">的了</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">There's </span></em></strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">nothing left to</span></em></strong> say.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">没有什么</strong>好说<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">的了</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">Nothing left to</span></em></strong> do but join your friends and dance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">除了和你的朋友们一起跳舞，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">别无他法</strong>。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>I <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">had nothing left to</span></em></strong> give, and that confused me.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">没有什么</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">可以</strong>给<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">的了</strong>，这让我很困惑。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">There's nothing left to</span></em></strong> do.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">没什么</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">可</strong>做<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">的了</strong>。<span style="text-align: center;font-size: 16px;"></span></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" way</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">学校目前<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">在各个方面</strong>都大有改善。</p><p from Ethan<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"> in every way</span></em></strong>, except one.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你和伊森<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">完全</strong>不同，除了一个方面。</p></section><section border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">   活学活用</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);padding: 0px 9px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">请用<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> have nothing left to.../ there is nothing left to...  </strong>随意造句</p></section></section></section></section></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;font-size: 16px;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">全文字数：   2258</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">阅读时间：   7 分钟</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">图片数目：   8</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin: 10px 0%;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 100 100 0%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgba(116, 185, 240, 0.79);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: 25px;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;align-self: center;line-height: 0;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: perspective(0px);-webkit-transform: perspective(0px);-moz-transform: perspective(0px);-o-transform: perspective(0px);transform-style: flat;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;justify-content: center;transform: rotateX(180deg);-webkit-transform: rotateX(180deg);-moz-transform: rotateX(180deg);-o-transform: rotateX(180deg);margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 10px;height: 10px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 10px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(255, 208, 90);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: auto;align-self: center;flex: 100 100 0%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgba(116, 185, 240, 0.79);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今天是2021年8月19日，到今天为止早读500天啦！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">时间过得好快，已经早读一年多了。这一年多里，在早读班认识了许多小伙伴，我们会一起探讨发音，探讨班级管理，聊生活的趣事～感谢关关老师让我们相聚在一起。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;white-space: nowrap;overflow: hidden;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(117, 114, 114);display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;line-height: 1.3;padding: 0px 0.2em;background-color: rgb(117, 114, 114);color: rgb(230, 229, 219);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 1 </p></section><section style="display: inline-block;padding: 0px 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">【自己的早读之路】</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">自己是从2019年4月6日加入早读的，一开始只是出于好奇和兴趣，当时加入的是186班。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当时也没有把早读当成每天第一件要做的事，只是简单的听一下老师的示范发音便打卡了。后面知道还有班长为自己免费纠音，便会尽量争取班长们的纠音，自己的发音也在慢慢提高。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一次机缘巧合下，参加了49班四周年庆，当时十分震撼，准备得<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">太用心啦</strong>！<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">氛围感</strong>也十足！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">周年庆结束后便申请留下观摩几天～</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">班级里的氛围非常打动我，不管是打卡的速度，还是大家互动的气氛，都非常好。于是自己不舍地告别了第一个早读班，来到了第49班。也曾经半开玩笑地说过这会是最后一个早读班，我相信会的🙈</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在49班里认识了可爱的学委们，班长们和同学们。非常开心能和你们认识和相遇。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">受到学委的感染，对早读我也更加上心了：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">每天醒来第一件事就是打开公众号，收听老师的早读讲解。也开始尝试预习，记笔记，写音标，把需要注意的发音点、词链儿、班长纠音统统记下来。<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">但缺少复盘，自己还需要多多地回顾。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;margin: 0px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;align-self: flex-end;flex: 60 60 0%;height: auto;margin: 0px 10px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(68, 73, 85);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(255, 206, 25);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">#</strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> 学习笔记</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: border-box;">音标课，口语课，语音课</strong><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;">，受益匪浅。</span><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;">其实有些知识老师在平时的早读里都有渗透，不过学课程会更系统，价格也很亲民，班长们也超级的认真负责。</span><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;">不是打广告</span><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;">噢🤪</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">“Good wine needs no bush.”</strong>🤗</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">真的很感谢关老师，可以让我遇到这么多优秀的人～</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.75" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfMBRicgibt2dumCQZz7vnxKiby7C18PNhesCsCM4dVYwqiaDlfR1iaNsMFwsLCmD788NKicB2ficib7udTXw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="512" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;white-space: nowrap;overflow: hidden;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(117, 114, 114);display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;line-height: 1.3;padding: 0px 0.2em;background-color: rgb(117, 114, 114);color: rgb(230, 229, 219);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 2 </p></section><section style="display: inline-block;padding: 0px 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">【自己的纠音之路】</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">记得自己是在19年7月参加的班长考核，并且顺利通过了，接下来便开启了实习生活，一共实习了99天。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这段时间里非常感谢师傅们对我的帮助，自己</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">从一开始的忐忑到后面的自如，</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">从不知道怎么做到慢慢有了头绪，</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">从不善表达到更加乐意表达自己......</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">真的打心底里感到喜悦，也让我更加严格地要求自己。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">期间担任了139班和86班的班长🤪之后我也成了别人的师傅，更加体会到<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">“教别人一碗水，你得有一桶水”</strong>的道理。说起来这是我第二次当师傅了。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">第一次是指导班长们的早读，但是对于他们的纠音并没有特别深入的去听。不过这次则是不光指导他们早读，还一个个指导他们的纠音。在这个过程中，也重新回顾了一些音标。感觉<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">“学无止境”</strong>，真的要<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">常回“课程”看看</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfMBRicgibt2dumCQZz7vnxKibA1iadxkIVLEJg2ekQIRT5eXtwxQy5EVbFkVyPBxVa683fQaW2vcDZPA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="355" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">同时自己读和纠别人读音又不太一样，首先自己要知道他的问题在哪，正确的音怎么读，然后你怎么样去教他，怎么样能让他理解。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">和老师早读版块每年都有更新一样，我的纠音也在<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">慢慢尝试简便又重点突出的方法</strong>。一开始是直接班群里一个一个纠，在本子上写下对应同学的学号，姓名，音系，以及他们发音的问题点，同时延续着实习以来的习惯，纠音完一定有一个小结。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">之后慢慢知道了怎么样笔记纠音，怎么样收藏同学们的语音条，然后一个个纠音。最近也借鉴了一些班班们的纠音模式，先统一详细的讲解个别单词和发音，再针对个人补充个别发音问题。这个过程中发现要把这些词和音说好，又能让人家理解，确实不是一件容易的事。<strong>还是要多多打磨自己的一些发音，而且多复盘。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">同时同学们的反馈对我们来说也是一种肯定，所以你们看到纠音后一定要有反应哦，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">不要让我们的纠音石沉大海</strong>～我们要双向奔赴嘛，对不对？🙊</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;white-space: nowrap;overflow: hidden;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(117, 114, 114);display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;line-height: 1.3;padding: 0px 0.2em;background-color: rgb(117, 114, 114);color: rgb(230, 229, 219);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 3 </p></section><section style="display: inline-block;padding: 0px 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">【自己的管理之路】</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;">2021年4月4日，我来到了早读37班，整体来说，班级早读的质量，氛围，班班们、同学们都挺不错，非常开心能和大家相遇。</span><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">学委的管理工作是比较纷繁复杂的，一天的工作有这么几项：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">督促同学打卡；</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">检查打卡序号；</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">检查截图；</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">抽听语音条，看会不会盲读；</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">到点了查找没有打卡的人，提醒他们该打卡了；</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">写小结；</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">周末整理考勤等等</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">......</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">虽然因人而异，但确实需要花一些精力。还需要协调各种关系，俨然是个<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">“班主任”</strong>了😆</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">时间久了，便会轻松一些，在这个过程中也可以学到很多东西，比如可以<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">积累到社群管理经验和社交经验</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7月3日我们举行了5周年庆，前后准备了一个月左右，再次感谢大家的参与，非常荣幸可以和大家一起见证5周年，希望我们可以一起度过第二个5周年😜</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">虽然在管理的过程中有时也会遇到一些小问题，但是大家还是非常的理解和支持，谢谢你们❤️</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: That's the secret to a fulfilling career.” </strong></a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: border-box;">今天的早读内容感触比较深～</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我觉得早读班的班委们应该拥有姓名～</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有些班委或擅长管理，或精通专业，在老师灯塔般的带领下，助人者自助，是双赢～</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">是啊！虽然班长纠音和学委管理都是公益的，但是我们却打心底里愿意跟随您，愿意和大家一起前行～这就是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">榜样的力量</strong>吧！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">还有很多句看似平常的话，在某些时刻真的可以给我们力量😘</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我想自己如此的喜欢关老师，喜欢这个平台，喜欢早读班的原因，还是在于关老师的</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: border-box;">今天是2021年8月19日，到今天为止早读500天啦！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">时间过得好快，已经早读一年多了。这一年多里，在早读班认识了许多小伙伴，我们会一起探讨发音，探讨班级管理，聊生活的趣事～感谢关关老师让我们相聚在一起。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;white-space: nowrap;overflow: hidden;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(117, 114, 114);display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;line-height: 1.3;padding: 0px 0.2em;background-color: rgb(117, 114, 114);color: rgb(230, 229, 219);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 1 </p></section><section style="display: inline-block;padding: 0px 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">【自己的早读之路】</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">自己是从2019年4月6日加入早读的，一开始只是出于好奇和兴趣，当时加入的是186班。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当时也没有把早读当成每天第一件要做的事，只是简单的听一下老师的示范发音便打卡了。后面知道还有班长为自己免费纠音，便会尽量争取班长们的纠音，自己的发音也在慢慢提高。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一次机缘巧合下，参加了49班四周年庆，当时十分震撼，准备得<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">太用心啦</strong>！<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">氛围感</strong>也十足！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">周年庆结束后便申请留下观摩几天～</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">班级里的氛围非常打动我，不管是打卡的速度，还是大家互动的气氛，都非常好。于是自己不舍地告别了第一个早读班，来到了第49班。也曾经半开玩笑地说过这会是最后一个早读班，我相信会的🙈</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在49班里认识了可爱的学委们，班长们和同学们。非常开心能和你们认识和相遇。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">受到学委的感染，对早读我也更加上心了：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">每天醒来第一件事就是打开公众号，收听老师的早读讲解。也开始尝试预习，记笔记，写音标，把需要注意的发音点、词链儿、班长纠音统统记下来。<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">但缺少复盘，自己还需要多多地回顾。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;margin: 0px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;align-self: flex-end;flex: 60 60 0%;height: auto;margin: 0px 10px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(68, 73, 85);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(255, 206, 25);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">#</strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> 学习笔记</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="7.162963" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfMBRicgibt2dumCQZz7vnxKibc1hppmVktU7cqialbyt0AwtSakFic2OsoydhD40Vk5GhWKZhGTNibggrg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" auto;flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: flex-end;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 20px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="7.2083333" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfMBRicgibt2dumCQZz7vnxKibnP0CrenQSmgCe388SumSK6Jfy8kBJJmepzWSBgbAn3I3ibG8PaiaSqEA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">假期<span style="letter-spacing: 0px;">期间报名了老师的</span><strong style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">音标课，口语课，语音课</strong><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;">，受益匪浅。</span><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;">其实有些知识老师在平时的早读里都有渗透，不过学课程会更系统，价格也很亲民，班长们也超级的认真负责。</span><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;">不是打广告</span><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;">噢🤪</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">“Good wine needs no bush.”</strong>🤗</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">真的很感谢关老师，可以让我遇到这么多优秀的人～</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.75" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfMBRicgibt2dumCQZz7vnxKiby7C18PNhesCsCM4dVYwqiaDlfR1iaNsMFwsLCmD788NKicB2ficib7udTXw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="512" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;white-space: nowrap;overflow: hidden;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(117, 114, 114);display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;line-height: 1.3;padding: 0px 0.2em;background-color: rgb(117, 114, 114);color: rgb(230, 229, 219);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 2 </p></section><section style="display: inline-block;padding: 0px 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">【自己的纠音之路】</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">记得自己是在19年7月参加的班长考核，并且顺利通过了，接下来便开启了实习生活，一共实习了99天。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这段时间里非常感谢师傅们对我的帮助，自己</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">从一开始的忐忑到后面的自如，</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">从不知道怎么做到慢慢有了头绪，</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">从不善表达到更加乐意表达自己......</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">真的打心底里感到喜悦，也让我更加严格地要求自己。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">期间担任了139班和86班的班长🤪之后我也成了别人的师傅，更加体会到<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">“教别人一碗水，你得有一桶水”</strong>的道理。说起来这是我第二次当师傅了。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">第一次是指导班长们的早读，但是对于他们的纠音并没有特别深入的去听。不过这次则是不光指导他们早读，还一个个指导他们的纠音。在这个过程中，也重新回顾了一些音标。感觉<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">“学无止境”</strong>，真的要<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">常回“课程”看看</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfMBRicgibt2dumCQZz7vnxKibA1iadxkIVLEJg2ekQIRT5eXtwxQy5EVbFkVyPBxVa683fQaW2vcDZPA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="355" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">同时自己读和纠别人读音又不太一样，首先自己要知道他的问题在哪，正确的音怎么读，然后你怎么样去教他，怎么样能让他理解。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">和老师早读版块每年都有更新一样，我的纠音也在<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">慢慢尝试简便又重点突出的方法</strong>。一开始是直接班群里一个一个纠，在本子上写下对应同学的学号，姓名，音系，以及他们发音的问题点，同时延续着实习以来的习惯，纠音完一定有一个小结。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">之后慢慢知道了怎么样笔记纠音，怎么样收藏同学们的语音条，然后一个个纠音。最近也借鉴了一些班班们的纠音模式，先统一详细的讲解个别单词和发音，再针对个人补充个别发音问题。这个过程中发现要把这些词和音说好，又能让人家理解，确实不是一件容易的事。<strong>还是要多多打磨自己的一些发音，而且多复盘。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">同时同学们的反馈对我们来说也是一种肯定，所以你们看到纠音后一定要有反应哦，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">不要让我们的纠音石沉大海</strong>～我们要双向奔赴嘛，对不对？🙊</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;white-space: nowrap;overflow: hidden;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(117, 114, 114);display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;line-height: 1.3;padding: 0px 0.2em;background-color: rgb(117, 114, 114);color: rgb(230, 229, 219);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 3 </p></section><section style="display: inline-block;padding: 0px 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">【自己的管理之路】</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;">2021年4月4日，我来到了早读37班，整体来说，班级早读的质量，氛围，班班们、同学们都挺不错，非常开心能和大家相遇。</span><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">学委的管理工作是比较纷繁复杂的，一天的工作有这么几项：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">督促同学打卡；</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">检查打卡序号；</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">检查截图；</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">抽听语音条，看会不会盲读；</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">到点了查找没有打卡的人，提醒他们该打卡了；</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">写小结；</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">周末整理考勤等等</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">......</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">虽然因人而异，但确实需要花一些精力。还需要协调各种关系，俨然是个<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">“班主任”</strong>了😆</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;height: auto;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 2px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="5.8425926" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfMBRicgibt2dumCQZz7vnxKibtL7iaxBd9usjrPrhaIeSL6SbI6U2COMhOM9wFafDMwswvR7diaN96YsA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">时间久了，便会轻松一些，在这个过程中也可以学到很多东西，比如可以<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">积累到社群管理经验和社交经验</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7月3日我们举行了5周年庆，前后准备了一个月左右，再次感谢大家的参与，非常荣幸可以和大家一起见证5周年，希望我们可以一起度过第二个5周年😜</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">虽然在管理的过程中有时也会遇到一些小问题，但是大家还是非常的理解和支持，谢谢你们❤️</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;white-space: nowrap;overflow: hidden;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(117, 114, 114);display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;line-height: 1.3;padding: 0px 0.2em;background-color: rgb(117, 114, 114);color: rgb(230, 229, 219);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 4 </p></section><section style="display: inline-block;padding: 0px 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">【写在结尾】</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2021年1月8日，早读内容是这句话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-linktype="2" href="https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653546134&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=5b7abf6bc14a65c494255c082cd6216c&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;" target="_blank"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">“Focus on getting good at something that genuinely helps others, and makes the world a better place. That's the secret to a fulfilling career.” </strong></a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;">（点击文本即可跳转早读页面）</span></em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我在老师微博底下的评论是：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今天的早读内容感触比较深～</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我觉得早读班的班委们应该拥有姓名～</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有些班委或擅长管理，或精通专业，在老师灯塔般的带领下，助人者自助，是双赢～</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">是啊！虽然班长纠音和学委管理都是公益的，但是我们却打心底里愿意跟随您，愿意和大家一起前行～这就是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">榜样的力量</strong>吧！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">还有很多句看似平常的话，在某些时刻真的可以给我们力量😘</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我想自己如此的喜欢关老师，喜欢这个平台，喜欢早读班的原因，还是在于关老师的</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">个人</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">魅力（认真负责谦逊）</strong>，</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">您的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">勤勉（每日一更，未曾停歇）</strong>，</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">您的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">生活态度（随心随性）</strong>！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">就像一位同学说的那样“您是一股清流”😜</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">感谢相遇！❤️</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">因为早读，吸引了许多和您同频的人，而我也荣幸的成为了一份子。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>让我们一起早读到老！</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A little effort every day, you will make a big difference!</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 2px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 4px;border-style: dashed;border-color: rgba(157, 187, 254, 0.46);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1" 62);background-color: rgb(255, 208, 90);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: auto;align-self: center;flex: 100 100 0%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgba(116, 185, 240, 0.79);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin:
