border-box;">（微信号teachergwen02）</strong><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">。一经采纳，将送出现已绝版的【早读纪念套卡】或【纪念刊】一套。</span><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">本栏目长期征稿，每周二发出。</span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.262963" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfMBRicgibt2dumCQZz7vnxKibptlQNBnyQ168ny1hPvOPTKibT0O8sCQR2uocIcjicqU3RaGaDazSnoBA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></sectio</section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1. peckish </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK&amp;US /ˈpekɪʃ/ adj. slightly hungry</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2. emergency </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/ɪˈmɜːdʒənsi/ US/ɪˈmɜːrdʒənsi/ noun </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">something dangerous or serious, such as an accident, that happens suddenly or unexpectedly and needs fast action in order to avoid harmful results紧急情况；不测事件；突发事件</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">【Collocations词语搭配】</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Verb处理紧急情况：deal with an emergency</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">cope with an emergency</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">handle an emergency </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Noun 紧急情况 an emergency situation      </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">紧急处理 emergency treatment（多用于医疗）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">紧急援助/救济/帮助 emergency aid/relief/help      </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">紧急会议 an emergency meeting/an emergency session </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">紧急手术 an emergency operation</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">应急措施 emergency measures</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">紧急权力 emergency powers</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">紧急车辆 an emergency vehicle(=an ambulance or fire engine)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Phrase: in case of emergency/in the event of an emergency (=if there is an emergency)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g.: The fire-exit doors should only be opened in case of emergency.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">只有在紧急情况下才能打开防火门。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3. makeshift </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK&amp;US/ˈmeɪkʃɪft/ adj. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">made to be used for a short time only when nothing better is available权宜的；临时代用的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g:Thousands of refugees are living in makeshift camps.数千个的难民居住在临时帐篷里。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4. humble </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK&amp;US/ˈhʌmbəl/ adj.  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">having a low social class or position 地位低下的，卑微的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5. temporary </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/ˈtempərəri,ˈtempəri/ US/ˈtempəreri/注意发音 adj. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">not lasting or needed for very long短暂的；暂时的，临时的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">【Thesaurus近义词辨析】</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Temporary----continuing for only a limited period of time仅在有限的时间内临时持续 </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">temporary staff 临时工</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a temporary visa 临时签证</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Provisional----used especially about arrangements or information that people may decide to change in the future. Also used about licences or governments which are only arranged to last for a short time特别用于人们可能决定在未来改变的安排或信息，也用于只安排持续很短时间的许可证或政府</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Does the hotel accept provisional bookings? 酒店接受临时预订吗？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They have set a provisional date for the next meeting.他们为下次会议定了一个临时日期。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a provisional driving licence临时驾驶执照</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a provisional government临时政府</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Stopgap[only before noun]----used about something that you use for a short time until you can replace it with something better权宜之计,用于您在短时间内使用的东西，直到您可以用更好的东西替换它</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We might have to employ someone temporarily as a stopgap measure until we can hire someone permanently.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在找到人填补这个空缺之前，我们可能得先暂时雇个人顶一下。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Passing[only before noun]----used about an interest, thought, or feeling that is short and not very serious用于表示短暂且不是很严重的兴趣、想法或感觉</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">As a student, I didn’t give working in finance even a passing thought.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">作为一名学生，我没有想过要从事金融工作。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Ephemeral----lasting for only a short time短暂的；极短的；转瞬即逝的，存在或流行的时间很短</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Fame in the world of rock and pop is largely ephemeral.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在摇滚和流行音乐界，名声大多转瞬即逝。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Many new words, particularly slang, are fleeting and ephemeral.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">许多新词，尤其是俚语，都是转瞬即逝的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Transient----continuing for only a limited time, or staying somewhere for only a short time – used especially to say that something is always changing, or people only stay somewhere for a short time只持续有限的时间，或只在某处停留很短的时间——特指某事总是在变化，或人们只在某处停留很短的时间</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the transient nature of life生命的短暂本质</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's an organization set up to provide money and help for transients.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个组织建立的目的就是给暂住者提供钱款和帮助。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Beijing has a highly transient population.北京的人口流动性很强。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6. I can't help feel all this is getting a little personal我不禁觉得这一切都变得有点私人化了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7. practical reason显示因素，实际原因，更实际的理由</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">8. there's no excuse for something 没有借口</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">used to say that someone’s behaviour is too bad to be explained or accepted 常用于说某人的行为太糟糕而无法解释或接受</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;margin-top: -3px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;background-color: rgb(232, 181, 181);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="border-top: 1px solid rgb(232, 181, 181);width: his vi<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ew<sup style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">(w)</sup> 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">这就是威尔逊刚刚说到的，我们吃午饭时就像遇到了紧急情况。这也说明了在英国，我们对待工作和食物的态度。接下来，我们来听听哲学家朱利安</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">·</span><span style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">"It is silent now. But I have stood here when the whole air was full of the noises of Charn; the trampling of feet, the creaking of wheels, the cracking of the whips and the groaning of slaves, the thunder of chariots, and the sacrificial drums beating in the temples. I have stood here (but that was near the end) when the roar of battle went up from every street and the river of Charn ran red." She paused and added, "All in one moment one woman blotted it out for ever."</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“现在很安静。但是当空中充斥着恰恩的各种声音那会儿，我曾站在这里。脚步声、车轮声、鞭子的抽打声和奴隶的呻吟，还有马车的轰响以及寺庙里献祭的鼓声。当战斗开始，每条街道上杀声四起，恰恩河水被鲜血染红的时候，我也曾站在这儿（但那时一切都快完了）。”停了一下，她又说，“一个女人顷刻间便将这一切永远地抹去了。”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 她太笨了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 谁管她笨不笨？她很漂亮。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 那又怎么样？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 你只不过是嫉妒罢了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: She is so stupid.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Who cares? She is pretty.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: So what?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: You're just jealous.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The ________ president was the youngest president ever in American history.</p><p 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> 1. potent adj. 有效力的；有影响力的；强大的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">近义词：powerful</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">potent </span></strong></em>drugs <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">强效</strong>药物/<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">猛</strong>药</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a very <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">potent</span></em></strong> alcoholic brew <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">烈性</strong>酒精饮料</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">potent</span></em></strong> argument <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">有力的</strong>论据</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">potent </span></em></strong>force <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">强大的</strong>力量</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">This is a very <span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">potent</span></em></strong> drug</span> and can have unpleasant <g style="box-sizing: border-box;">side-effects</g>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">该药<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">效力很强</strong>，副作用也不小。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. spice n. 调剂品；额外的刺激（或趣味）</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">herbs and <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">spices</span></em></strong> 香草和<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">香料</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">spice</span></em></strong> to our lives</span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们需要一次新奇的旅行来<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">调剂</strong>一下生活。</p><p style="white-space: 一撮；少量</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链儿：a pinch of XX 一小撮...</strong></p><p style="white-space: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">加<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">一撮</strong>盐来调味。</p></section><section style="z-index: 2;transform: translate(350.547px, 1782.89px);-webkit-transform: translate(350.547px, 1782.89px);-moz-transform: translate(350.547px, 1782.89px);-o-transform: translate(350.547px, 1782.89px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. 词链儿：dull one's senses 让人麻木</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">dull v. 使麻木，使迟钝    adj. 无趣的，枯燥的，沉闷的</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">dull XX  减轻...；（使）...变麻木</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Her fear and anxiety <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">dulled</span></em></strong> her mind.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">恐惧和焦虑使她的头脑<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">变得麻木</strong>了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The tablets they gave him <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">dulled</span></em></strong> the pain for a while.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们给他的药片暂时<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">缓解了</strong>疼痛。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>wake XX up &amp; dull one's senses 含义相反</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">让人清醒 &amp; 让人麻木</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>We forfeit a lot when we <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">dull </span></em></strong>our experience of the body.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当我们对身体的体验<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">变得迟钝</strong>时，我们失去了很多。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>What happens if we try to mask or <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">dull</span></em></strong> our fears?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">如果我们试图掩盖或<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">减弱</strong>我们的恐惧，会发生什么呢？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">dulls</span></em></strong> the senses. It keeps you <g style="box-sizing: border-box;">prisoner </g>here.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">它会让人<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">迷失</strong>心智，让你永远留在这儿。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">u·ti·li·tar·ian </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˌjuːtɪlɪˈteəriən  / </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 有效用的;实用的，功利(主义)的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 功利主义者;实用主义者</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">In expository prose, paragraphs can (and should) be neat and utilitarian.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">写说明文的时候，段落可以（并且应该是）简洁实用。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">So, the utilitarian position is in the middle.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">因此功利主义的立场是中立的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">at·tract·ive </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ əˈtræktɪv /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She's very intelligent. And she's attractive, too.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她很聪明，也很迷人。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Which is a very attractive design element.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这种设计很惹人注目。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">stuck</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v.刺（stick的过去式）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 不能动的；被卡住的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Without confidence, we get stuck, and when we get stuck, we can't even get started.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">如果没有信心，我们会陷入困境，当我们陷入困境时，我们甚至无法开始。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">My hand's stuck in the garbage disposal!</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我的手卡在食物垃圾处理机里了！</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">func·tion·al </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈfʌŋkʃənl /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 有用的, 实用的,能起作用的, 产生影响的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">At least your leg's fully functional.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你的腿起码还能行动自如。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The two natural aft lavatories are both functional.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那儿的两个盥洗室还都很好用。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">con·struct </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ kənˈstrʌkt/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v.建造，构造</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Why were the Viking churches constructed from wood?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">为什么维京教堂是用木头建造的？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A famous architect constructed a model of a new cathedral.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一位著名建筑师建造了一座新教堂模型。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">managed to 设法、努力（完成某事）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He managed to ward off the blow.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他设法避过了那一击。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">em·brace </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ɪmˈbreɪs/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. &amp; vi. 拥抱</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 包括; 包含,接受,信奉, 皈依</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 拥抱, 怀抱</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They embraced and promised to keep in touch. 他们互相拥抱，许诺将保持联系。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I saw China embracing the world and vice versa.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我看到中国在拥抱这个世界，而世界也进一步的接受中国。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">be aware of 知道，意识到…</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Be aware of what's going on around you.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">留意你周围发生了什么。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">hug</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/hʌg/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 紧抱；拥抱；抱有，坚持</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 拥抱；紧抱在一起；挤在一起</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 紧抱；拥抱；固执</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A hug always makes you feel better.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一个拥抱总会让你感觉更好。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">wrap </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ræp /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 包；隐藏；缠绕；掩护</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 缠绕；穿外衣；包起来</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 外套；围巾</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She wrapped her shawl closer about her.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她用披肩紧裹住身体</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">phys·ic·al </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈfɪzɪkl /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> adj. 身体的；物质的；物理的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 体格检查</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">physical fitness 健康体魄</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">physical appearance 外貌</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Exercise helps both mental and physical health.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">锻炼有助于身心健康</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">broaden our horizon 开阔视野; 扩宽视野</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Visiting museums could help broaden our horizon.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">参观博物馆可以拓宽我们的视野。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">broad·en </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈbrɔːdən/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 变宽，加宽；扩大，变阔</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 使变宽；使扩大</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">ho·ri·zon </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ həˈraɪzn/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 地平线；眼界；范围；视野</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">col·league </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈkɒliːɡ ; ˈkɑːliːɡ/</p><p It normally means this… let me just…</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">是的。我们看看这个词</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">embrace</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">，通常情况下这是指</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">……</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">让我想想。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: Oh Nei<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">l, I</span></span> didn'<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> know you cared. Neil jus<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> hugged me, wrapped hi<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span>rm<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span>roun<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">尼尔，我不知道你居然介意这个。尼尔，拥抱我，将胳膊环绕我，拥抱我。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: a</span></span>s we ca<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n e</span></span>mbrace physical things an<span I'm stuffed.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: What's the matter? It doesn't taste good?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: It's not that I don't like your cooking, but I ate some cookies before we had dinner.</p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. maybe w</strong><span style="color: 0);text-decoration: underline;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">e are</strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> 本句中的are不缩约不弱读；</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 语调参考：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">However it works,↗ </strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">when you find each other,↗ </strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.ditch  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/dɪtʃ/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to stop having something because you no longer want it</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">中文释义：v.抛弃；摆脱；丢弃；n.沟；渠</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Let's ditch school and go to the park.让我们逃学去公园吧。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.Vietnamese </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˌvjetnəˈmiːz◂/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">中文释义：n.越南人；越南语adj.越南的；越南人的；越南语的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3.Brit  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/brɪt/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">someone from Britain英国人=the British</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4.crying shame奇耻大辱；太可惜了</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">it’s a crying shame</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">释义：used to say that something is very sad or upsetting</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It would be a crying shame if high ticket prices kept people away from baseball games.如果高门票价格让人们远离棒球比赛，那将是一件令人遗憾的事。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5. run over v.轧过；碾过；演练；排练</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6.peckish  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈpekɪʃ/ adj.有点饿的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She was feeling a bit peckish.她有点儿饿。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7.makeshift  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈmeɪkʃɪft/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.权宜之计；临时替代品adj.临时的；凑合的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">8.goalkeeper </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈɡəʊlˌkiːpə $ ˈɡoʊlˌkiːpər/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.守门员；门将=goalie /ˈɡəʊli $ ˈɡoʊ-/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">9.bin  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/bɪn/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v.扔掉；丢弃n.垃圾箱；（有盖）大容器</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">steel bin 钢桶；铁桶</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">10.utilitarian </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/juːˌtɪləˈteəriən $ -ˈter-/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：intended to be useful and practical rather than attractive or comfortable</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">中文释义：n.功利主义者adj.实用的；功利的；实惠的；功利主义的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">11.functional</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈfʌŋkʃənəl/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj.实用的；作用的；功能的；机能的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The company was divided into four main functional areas.该公司被划分为四个主要职能领域。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: I shoul<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(75, 172, 198);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> ditch my sandwich <span style="color: rgb(247, 150, 70);box-sizing: border-box;">and</span> eat with you. In the na<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">me o</span></span>f team spirit – tha<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t i</span></span>s – gettin<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">g o</span></span>n well with team members – having a feelin<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">g o</span></span>f belonging.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我明白了。我应该扔掉我的三明治，和你一起吃饭。团队精神是指团队成员之间相处融洽，有归属感。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: Finally. Vietnamese?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">所以，一起吃越南菜？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: Oh yes, bu<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(75, 172, 198);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> no<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(75, 172, 198);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> before you tell me th<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">e a</span></span>nswer to today's question. How long do Brits take for lunch?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">好的，但你得先告诉我今天问题的答案。英国人吃午餐的平均时长？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: Well th<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">e a</span></span>nswer was c) 25 minutes. Tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(75, 172, 198);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> comes fro<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">m a</span></span> survey done by the BBC this year to fin<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d ou</span></span>t abou<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(75, 172, 198);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> our modern dining habits.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">答案是</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">c) 25</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">分钟。今年，</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">BBC</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">为了研究现代饮食习惯做了一项调查，这一数据就来自自此项调查。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: 25 minutes? I<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t's a</span></span> crying shame, Dan. But before we have lunch ourselves, let's ru<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n o</span></span>ver the vocabulary one more time.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">只有</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">25</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">分钟？这真是奇耻大辱。在吃午饭前，我们再次回顾一下今天的单词。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: Firs<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t u</span></span>p we had peckish. It means hungry – just a little hungry. I'm feeling rather pecki<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">sh a</span></span>t the moment.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">首先我们提到了</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">peckish</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">。</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">peckish</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">的意思是饥饿的，有点饿。我现在感到很饿，你呢？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: I think I've gone beyond peckish, Dan. Ro<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ll o</span></span>n lunch. Next?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我觉得我现在已经饿过劲了。继续，下一个是？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: We had makeshift – which describes a temporary or low quality solution. Fo<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">r e</span></span>xample, last week my team's goalkeeper wa<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s s</span></span>ick, so I had to replace him a<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span> makeshift goalie.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">makeshift</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">描述的是临时的，低品质的解决办法。例如，上周我们队的守门员病了，所以我不得不作为临时守门员来替代他。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: Or, anothe<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">r e</span></span>xample – whe<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n I</span></span> was a student I used the steel bi<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n i</span></span>n my room as a makeshift drum.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">另一个例子，在我还是个学生时，我把房间里的钢桶用作临时鼓。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: I'm sure the neighbour love<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(75, 172, 198);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> that. Now wha<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t a</span></span>bout this word utilitarian? In the context we use<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d i</span></span>t, it means simple and functional, rather than beautiful.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我相信你的邻居们很喜欢。现在我们来谈谈</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">“</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">功利主义的</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">”</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">这个词。在我们使用的语境中，它是指简单的，实用的，但并不美好。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: Do you think i<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(75, 172, 198);box-sizing: border-box;">t </span></span>woul<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(75, 172, 198);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> be fair to describe your polo shirt as utilitarian?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">你觉得用它来描述你的</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Polo</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">衫怎么样呢？</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Then their heads came out of the pool and, once more, the sunny quietness of the Wood between the Worlds was all about them, and it seemed richer and warmer and more peaceful than ever after the staleness and ruin of the place they had just left. I think that, if they had been given the chance, they would again have forgotten who they were and where they came from and would have lain down and enjoyed themselves, half asleep, listening to the growing of the trees.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">脑袋一出水潭，他们便再次来到各个世界之间的树林，置身于阳光明媚的宁静之中。刚刚离开那个陈腐、荒芜的地方，这片树林似乎比以前更显得青翠、温暖和安详。我想，如果可能的话，他们又会忘记自己是谁，从哪儿来，然后躺下，聆听树木的生长，朦朦胧胧地享受快乐。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 或许你该跟老师谈谈。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 不，那没用。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 除非你试，否则你永远不知道。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我知道。她不可能更改我的分数。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Maybe you should talk to the teacher. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: No, it's no use. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: You never know unless you try. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I know. She won't change my grade. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Kara _________ the bottle, and the water rushed out.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">卡拉挤压着那个瓶子,水一下子喷了出来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. keep doing XX 持续/重复做...</strong></p><p style="text-align: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">keep telling</span></strong></em> you, but you won’t listen!</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">一再</strong>跟你说，但你就是不肯听！</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><em><strong>Keep smiling</strong></em></span>! <strong>要保持笑容</strong>！</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→keep cherishing one's old knowledge 保持对旧知识的珍惜/珍爱 → 温故</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 14px;">“温故”没有使用常见的review等词，译者理雅各（James Legge）选用“cherish”含有“珍爱、珍惜”的意思；汉学家亚瑟·威利译选用“reanimate”具有“使得老的知识获得新的力量”的意思。</span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></em></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>2. cherish v. 珍爱；怀念</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">Cherish</span></em></strong> the memory of those days in Paris.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">怀念</strong>在巴黎的岁月。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. →acquire  (one's) new (knowledge)  获得新的知识→ 知新</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: border-box;">acquire knowledge</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">老师应该教导学生怎么去<strong style="box-sizing: 为了持续不断地做某事</strong></p><p style="font-size: 14px;text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="font-size: 14px;text-align: 39);box-sizing: border-box;">o as not to</span></em></strong> disturb anyone.</p><p style="font-size: 14px;text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);padding: 0px 17px;text-shadow: rgb(183, 130, 204) 1px 1px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">03</em></strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;border-width: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);flex: 0 0 auto;align-self: flex-end;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 15px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 10px 10px 0px 0px;border-style: style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: auto;vertical-align: bottom;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 0px 0px 10px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: flex-end;height: auto;background-color: rgb(199, 187, 204);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: -5px 0% 6px;transform: translate3d(6px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(6px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(6px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(6px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);letter-spacing: 2px;line-height: 1;padding: 0px 20px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">看词链</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大家在片段中找到今天的主题表达了吗？Emily跟好友在对话的一开始抱怨了一会儿法国人，然后转入正题之前，说了一句: <span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I'll get down to brass tacks. 我们说正事吧！当我们在寒暄之后想要切入对话主题；言归正传的时候，就可以用这个表达啦。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</span></strong><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">：</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Come on! Let's just <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">get down to brass tacks</strong>. How much money do you need this time？</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">行了吧! 你就<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">开门见山</strong>吧，你这次要多少钱？</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I’m afraid I can give you only ten minutes’ time. <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Let’s get down to brass tacks at once.</strong><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>我恐怕只能给你十分钟，我们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">马上就谈正经的事吧</strong>!<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句3</strong>：<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>After the usual greetings and some remarks about the weather, the men<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> got down to brass tacks</strong>.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>在一般的问候以及几句关于天气的话后，那些人<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">就开始办正事</strong>了。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句4</strong>：<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>I do not come here to listen to your silly jokes. <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Let’s get down to brass tacks </strong>and decide on a schedule for our work.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>我不是来听你这些无聊的笑话的，让我们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">言归正传</strong>，订一个工作日程!</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">切入转正题还可以有哪些表达呢？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" href="http://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653553988&amp;idx=4&amp;sn=556dc7e5318a61396175aaccb9193496&amp;chksm=f7ebc589c09c4c9f3d7c05b9886e2582596dad162a8be60b369cfbda7d7f23c68c46826b349e&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="cut to the chase 切入正题"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;">cut to the chase 切入正题</span></strong></a><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"></span></strong></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">All right. So let's <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">cut to the chase</strong>. Who will be getting the checks, and when will they get them?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">好。我们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">直接切入正题</strong>吧。谁能得到支票，何时能得到？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Anyway 不管怎样</strong></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Anyway</strong>, both of these girls are into you; take your pick.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">说正事，</strong>这两个女孩都很喜欢你 你挑吧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链</strong>：long to 非常想XX</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：I <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">l<span style="box-sizing: border-box;">onged </span>to</strong> pierce his armour of complete indifference. 我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">恨不得</strong>一下子刺穿了他那副冷漠的甲胄。</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>：Try having a name like Robertson. Every French person<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> dry heaves</strong> just trying to pronounce it.</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链</strong>：dry heaves 干呕</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：The cold made my <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">dry heave</strong>. 感冒的时候我会干<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">呕</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width:
