border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 15px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 10px 10px 0px 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);background-color: rgb(199, 187, 204);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: auto;vertical-align: bottom;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 0px 0px 10px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);flex: 100 100 0%;align-self: flex-end;height: auto;background-color: rgb(199, 187, 204);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: -5px 0% 6px;transform: translate3d(6px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(6px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(6px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(6px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);letter-spacing: 2px;line-height: 1;padding: 0px 20px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">看词链</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大家在片段中找到今天的主题表达了吗？Emily跟好友在对话的一开始抱怨了一会儿法国人，然后转入正题之前，说了一句: <span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I'll get down to brass tacks. 我们说正事吧！当我们在寒暄之后想要切入对话主题；言归正传的时候，就可以用这个表达啦。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</span></strong><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">：</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Come on! Let's just <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">get down to brass tacks</strong>. How much money do you need this time？</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">行了吧! 你就<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">开门见山</strong>吧，你这次要多少钱？</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I’m afraid I can give you only ten minutes’ time. <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Let’s get down to brass tacks at once.</strong><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>我恐怕只能给你十分钟，我们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">马上就谈正经的事吧</strong>!<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句3</strong>：<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>After the usual greetings and some remarks about the weather, the men<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> got down to brass tacks</strong>.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>在一般的问候以及几句关于天气的话后，那些人<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">就开始办正事</strong>了。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句4</strong>：<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>I do not come here to listen to your silly jokes. <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Let’s get down to brass tacks </strong>and decide on a schedule for our work.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>我不是来听你这些无聊的笑话的，让我们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">言归正传</strong>，订一个工作日程!</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">切入转正题还可以有哪些表达呢？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" href="http://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653553988&amp;idx=4&amp;sn=556dc7e5318a61396175aaccb9193496&amp;chksm=f7ebc589c09c4c9f3d7c05b9886e2582596dad162a8be60b369cfbda7d7f23c68c46826b349e&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="cut to the chase 切入正题"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;">cut to the chase 切入正题</span></strong></a><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"></span></strong></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">All right. So let's <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">cut to the chase</strong>. Who will be getting the checks, and when will they get them?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">好。我们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">直接切入正题</strong>吧。谁能得到支票，何时能得到？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Anyway 不管怎样</strong></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Anyway</strong>, both of these girls are into you; take your pick.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">说正事，</strong>这两个女孩都很喜欢你 你挑吧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>：Sometimes I just <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">long to</strong> hear that r sound.</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链</strong>：long to 非常想XX</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：I <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">l<span style="box-sizing: border-box;">onged </span>to</strong> pierce his armour of complete indifference. 我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">恨不得</strong>一下子刺穿了他那副冷漠的甲胄。</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>：Try having a name like Robertson. Every French person<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> dry heaves</strong> just trying to pronounce it.</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链</strong>：dry heaves 干呕</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：The cold made my <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">dry heave</strong>. 感冒的时候我会干<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">呕</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.506" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/L4LJPfaSIKemxYKCEPdYtSdqbGmCarPetULmtYdsPe2CR7dArlAtTTxSFub3CIIKC64BtEibpMTpzHj5oFRLn6Q/640?wx_fmt=gif" data-type="gif" data-w="500" style="vertical-align: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>：I mean, it's gonna be a big<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> to-do</strong>. </p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链:</strong> to-do 忙乱；喧嚷；吵吵嚷嚷</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：What <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">a to-do</strong>! 真是太<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">大惊小怪</strong>了。</p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary &amp; Phrase</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.prefer  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ prɪˈfɜː(r)  ; NAmE prɪˈfɜːr  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v.较喜欢；喜欢…多于…</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：to like one thing or person better than another; to choose one thing rather than sth else because you like it better</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I prefer my coffee black. 我喜欢不加奶的咖啡。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.timeless   </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈtaɪmləs  ; NAmE ˈtaɪmləs  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj.不受时间影响的；无时间性的；永不过时的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：not appearing to be affected by the passing of time or by changes in fashion</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">her timeless beauty 她的永恒的美丽</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3.banter  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈbæntə(r)  ; NAmE ˈbæntər  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.（善意的）玩笑，打趣</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：friendly remarks and jokes</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He enjoyed exchanging banter with the customers. 他喜欢和顾客开玩笑。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He bantered with reporters and posed for photographers. 他和记者们打趣，并摆姿势让他们拍照。(作v.使用)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4.get along  相处; 相处融洽</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Humans and elephants don't always get along.人类和大象并不总能和睦相处。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5.stick with  继续做；坚持；保持联系</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Sounds scary, but stick with me here.听起来很吓人，但你听我说。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6.metaphorical  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˌmetəˈfɒrɪkl  ; NAmE ˌmetəˈfɔːrɪkl  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj.隐喻的；含比喻的；比喻性的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：connected with or containing metaphors</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Gentlemen, please. Leonard is trying to walk a mile in my metaphorical shoes.各位先生，莱纳德想" 穿我的鞋" 体验一下我的处境。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7.Even better  更胜一筹</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Or even better, get yourself off to a restaurant.下馆子更好。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;margin-top: -3px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;background-color: rgb(232, 181, 181);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="border-top: 1px solid rgb(232, 181, 181);width: 99.9%;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="text-align: right;margin: -1.1em 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, you've broadened your horizons.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">看起来你已经拓宽了眼界。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: Well, whe<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n I</span></span> taught English in Spain, Japan, Polan<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d an</span></span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> really broa<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">dened</span></em> my horizons an<span 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> new way<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s o</span></span>f life. Ho<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">w a</span></span>bou<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> you?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">在西班牙、日本、波兰和捷克共和国教英语的经历真的拓宽了我的眼界，还教会了我新的生活方式。你呢？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> certainly broa<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">dened</span></em> my horizons too.</span></p><p style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我们为什么不一起去旅行呢，和所有的英语学习团队一起去旅行？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span Tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> woul<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> be wonderful for team spiri<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> –the goo<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> feeli<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ng o</span></span>f being together. Maybe to Cambodia?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">对啊！这一定有助于增强团队精神。团队精神是指一起工作时的美好感觉。也许可以一起去柬埔寨？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: I<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> cer<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">tain</span></em>ly woul<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span>. style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">"You?" said the Queen in a still more terrible voice. Then, in one stride, she crossed the room, seized a great handful of Uncle Andrew's grey hair and pulled his head back so that his face looked up into hers. Then she studied his face as she had studied Digory's face in the palace of Charn. He blinked and licked his lips nervously all the time. At last she let him go: so suddenly that he reeled back against the wall.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“你！”女王的声青越加可怕。说着，她一步跨进屋子，一把抓住安德鲁舅舅的灰发，将他的头朝后一拧，使他的脸对着自己。然后，她像在恰恩王宫早研究迪格雷的脸一样仔细研究他的脸。他很紧张，不停地眨眼睛、舔嘴唇。最后，她松开手，他一下往后倒去，摇摇晃晃地撞在墙上。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你常去看体育比赛吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我家附近有比赛时，偶尔去看。但我通常看电视里的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你还能忆起这些比赛吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 有的能记住。但我永远都忘不了我们中国女排赢得世界杯的那场比赛。那是我看过的最惊心动魄的比赛。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Do you often go to watch sports games?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I go occasionally when there's a game on near home, but usually I watch it on TV.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Can you recall the games?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Sometimes. But I'll never forget the game in which our Chinese Women's Volleyball Team won the World Cup. It is the most thrilling and exciting game I have ever seen.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">After much delay, the results of the survey were published.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">耽搁多时之后,调查结果终于________了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">公布</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:
